---
layout: lexeme
lexeme: Kansanpuolue
---

###  Kansanpuolue₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Kansanpuolue* (people's party)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  48
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  ORG
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
